At the same time, Mr. Zhu was invited to report on the recent situation in the Northeast and the situation at the front lines. More than 100 representatives from more than 60 trade unions attended. The details are recorded below:

More than 100 representatives from more than 60 trade unions, including the Shipping Timber Industry, Nanhuo, No. 1 District Water and Electricity, Transportation, Gangpian, No. 1 District Paper Making, Shanghai-Ningbo Shipping Staff, No. 4 District Cigarette Rolling, No. 9 District Soap and Medicine, No. 7 District Cotton Weaving, Postal Workers, Pharmaceutical Industry, Sauce Industry, No. 6 District Water and Electricity, No. 1 District Shipbuilding, No. 5 District Cotton Spinning, Military Uniforms, No. 10 District Cotton Spinning, No. 4 District Water and Electricity, etc., including Zhu Xuefan, Ye Xianggao, Shao Xubai, Li Yongxiang, Lu Jiyun, Huang Jiabang, Zhou Xuexiang, Li Mengnan, Li Hua, Shen Jiabin, Ma Liqing, Zhao Zhenhui, Qi Jiamo, and others, attended the meeting.

The chairman gave a speech. First, Chairman Zhu Xuefan gave a speech, stating that General Zhu was entrusted by various groups in the city to preside over the work of providing relief to the volunteer armies in Peiping, which was quite arduous. General Zhu is old but still does not hesitate to endure hardship and work for the country. His noble character and passionate spirit of saving the country are admirable. This time, we should welcome him back to Shanghai. We are especially fortunate that General Zhu has graciously come to visit us.

Mr. Zhu gave a report. Then, Mr. Zhu Ziqiao gave a report, stating that the enemy forces in the Northeast are destroying everything. The volunteer armies are fighting with great difficulty. This has also been recorded in the newspapers, so I will not repeat it. The enemy forces' methods are extremely cruel. For example, in the Battle of Pingdingshan, some people fled to the top of the mountain, and the enemy forces pretended to say that the volunteer armies had retreated, luring the people down the mountain and machine-gunning them, leaving no one alive. The volunteer armies in the Northeast are still unwilling to surrender and are fighting fiercely with the tyrannical Japanese, such as Lao Beifeng and others who are particularly brave. Japan uses Manchukuo banknotes exclusively to buy goods at high prices, and refuses to use other banknotes from the Zhengjin, Taiwan, and other banks. This is because the Manchukuo banknotes have nothing to do with them. If the bank closes down one day, they can ignore it. Also, when fighting, they always use the puppet Manchu army as the front line, while the tyrannical army uses machine guns and artillery to suppress them from behind, causing the Chinese to kill each other. I have seen a map of puppet Manchuria drawn by the Japanese, which distinguishes all the provinces and regions only by different shades of color, including Suiyuan, Chahar, Inner and Outer Mongolia, and Hebei, which shows that their ambition to expand their territory is endless. The national army at various passes of the Great Wall, such as Song Zheyuan, Shang Zhen, Wang Yizhe, He Zhuguo, Sun Dianying, and others, are extremely brave. The only difficulty is the unevenness of the roads and the inconvenience of transportation. The front line needs at least heavy-duty trucks. The troops stationed at various passes currently need at least 700 heavy-duty trucks. Because there are no trucks, the horse-drawn carriages in Peiping and Tianjin have been requisitioned. However, now is the busy farming season, and mules and horses are urgently needed. If there are trucks, some of the donkeys and horses can be released back so that the farmers can cultivate the land. Now the troops are stationed in barren mountains and fields, and they have no way to buy the items they need, so they urgently need relief items. Our purpose is to provide relief as long as they can resist Japan, whether they are volunteer armies or the national army.

Sharp Decline in the Transportation of Japanese Goods to Hankou 139

The Owner of Baihualou Was Assassinated

Those Who Sell Japanese Goods Are Panicking

Japanese Merchants Are in a Difficult Situation

According to yesterday's Japanese Shanghai Daily, at 10:00 AM on the 4th, two people suddenly came to the Baihualou stationery store at the entrance of Huafeng Lane, Zhengjie, Wuchang, to meet with the store owner, Mr. Qian. After talking for a while, he was assassinated. The murderers escaped from the scene. After an investigation by various parties, Baihualou has a close relationship with a certain Japanese foreign firm and specializes in selling Japanese paper. He had recently received a warning from the Anti-Traitor Group, but Mr. Qian ignored it, so he suffered today's misfortune. Since the Wuhan National Goods Promotion Committee organized an investigation team, the goods transported from the Japanese Qing Company's warehouse have been strictly monitored. Therefore, Japanese merchants have been in an unprecedented predicament. The cargo carried by the Japanese Qing Shipping Company from March 25 to April 3, a total of four voyages, averaged about 125 tons of imported goods per voyage and no more than 50 tons of exported goods. The Luoyang Maru, which departed on April 3, imported only 15 tons of goods and exported only 4 tons of goods, which is an unprecedented record.

Minutes of the General Meeting of Shareholders of the Bank of China 140

Dividends Distributed According to Regulations, Net Profit 7%

Zhang Jia'ao, Li Ming, and Others Were Elected as Directors

The Bank of China held its 16th annual general meeting of shareholders at the Bankers' Association on Hong Kong Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. 576 shareholders attended, holding 116,962 shares, all of which met the legal quorum. The meeting was presided over by Chairman Li Fuxun, and the ceremony was held as usual. First, the chairman gave an opening speech and reported on the business situation in 1932. The net profit was 1,847,949.62 yuan. Then, Lu Xuepu, the representative of the Board of Supervisors, reported on the final accounts for 1932. Then, the plan for the distribution of profits for 1932 was discussed. The bank's total net profit was 1,847,949.62 yuan. According to regulations, one-tenth of the total net profit was set aside as a public reserve, totaling 184,794.96 yuan. The government shares were entitled to a 7% dividend, totaling 350,000 yuan. The commercial shares were entitled to a 7% dividend, totaling 1,379,819 yuan. Compared with the remaining net profit, there was a shortfall of more than 600,000 yuan, which was made up from the carry-over items. All of the above proposals were passed as they were. The term of office of the bank's directors had expired after four years and should be re-elected at this shareholders' meeting. In addition to the official shares, which were represented by Chief Xu Keting, who reported that the Ministry of Finance had appointed Ye Zhuotang, Li Qingquan, and Xi Demao as directors, the commercial shares were elected according to regulations. As a result of the vote, Li Ming, Zhang Jia'ao, Xu Chenmian, Bian Shousun, Chen Huide, Song Hanzhang, Rong Zongjin, Feng Gengguang, Zhou Zuomin, Pei Zuyi, Zhou Liang, and Kong Xiangxi were elected as commercial directors with the most votes.

Rally Declaration 149

The rally declaration states: Our country now has only two ways to deal with the tyrannical Japanese. If these two ways are not taken, the country and the nation will have no room to exist. The first way is to use military force to counterattack and drive the Japanese army out of our country. This is the business of our government, because our country already has funds for military expenses and already has two million troops. As long as the senior officers exert their previous courage to fight privately, they will be able to give the Japanese army serious lessons, just like the 19th Route Army, the 5th Army, and the 29th Army, to achieve our goal of eliminating foreign invaders. The second way is to use national products to counterattack and eliminate inferior Oriental goods from our country's market. This is the business of our people. Now there are many people who complain about our compatriots who sell Japanese goods and complain about the financial industry for accommodating Japanese goods merchants. We believe that all compatriots will not sell Japanese goods, and any financial industry that does not have a Jewish taste will not accommodate Japanese goods merchants. But what about us? Try to ask yourselves if you have a desire to take advantage of cheap Japanese goods? Can you not buy foreign goods that are suspected of being Japanese goods? Do you dislike the properties of national products that seem expensive and dislike their prices because they are not as good as foreign goods? We do not want to judge our gentlemen compatriots with the heart of a villain, but the facts tell us that the above questions cannot all be answered negatively. But we must know that the reason why Japanese goods are cheap is because our national goods exist, otherwise they must be expensive. The reason why Japanese goods pretend to be foreign goods or are managed by non-Japanese merchants is to see the effectiveness of our resistance. The counterattack of national goods against Japanese goods will surely succeed. We hope that our government will mobilize to eliminate the Japanese invaders within our borders, but we should also mobilize ourselves, use national goods to counterattack, eliminate Japanese goods within our borders, and strengthen our defenses. We should break off relations with those who sell Japanese goods and those who help sell Japanese goods. We should not communicate with them. We should use, introduce, and support national products, so that their production costs are low and their sales markets are wide. If this is the case, the government plans for the top, for military counterattacks, and the people plan for the bottom, for national products counterattacks, both sides work together to turn the tide. The tyrannical Japanese are not enough to be our enemy. This is a special declaration.

The Right to Send and Receive Telegrams for the Three Water and Electricity Companies Will Be Received Within Days 151

-The Ministry of Communications Has Issued an Order-

Regarding the right to directly send and receive telegrams in China for the Great Northern, Great Eastern, and Pacific Three Water and Electricity Companies, the Ministry of Communications has now negotiated to recover them.

Pan Chengjiong, Sun Xichen, and Li Jiqing have been appointed as the directors of receiving and sending for the Great Northern, Great Eastern, and Pacific Companies, and the International Telegraph Bureau has been ordered to receive the telegraph receiving and sending offices set up by the three companies in Shanghai as soon as possible. As of last night, the International Telegraph Bureau had not received this order. According to reliable sources, the order has been issued by the Ministry of Communications and will arrive in Shanghai soon. Therefore, the right of the three companies to directly send and receive telegrams in China will be implemented within a few days. According to the Greater America Evening News, Mr. Fulton, the manager of the Great Eastern Telegraph Company in Shanghai, said that the new submarine cable contract signed by the Great Northern, Pacific, and Great Eastern Companies and the Ministry of Communications is very satisfactory. The consultations between the two parties have been going on for a long time. The recent resumption of negotiations has been welcomed by all parties. Now that the contract has been signed, the business of receiving and sending telegrams will be transferred to the Chinese Telegraph Bureau, and the company has obtained satisfactory guarantees to maintain its efficiency and existing standards. Therefore, both parties are completely satisfied with this contract. After being accepted by the headquarters of the three companies, it was signed on the 5th of this month. According to the current contract, the three companies recognize Chinese sovereignty, but their activities in Shanghai can be extended for fourteen years. After the business of receiving and sending telegrams is transferred, a Westerner will still be assigned to assist the Chinese director in management. The contents of the contract include: (1) Abolishing the previous landing rights granted to the three companies, (2) Stipulating the landing years of submarine cables, (3) The Ministry of Communications recovering the right to directly send and receive telegrams, (4) Revising the percentage of income from submarine cable services received by the Chinese government, (5) Recovering land cables and overhead lines, (6) The Tianjin-Peiping-Gugou line will also be received by the government, (7) Abolishing the Shanghai-Hong Kong submarine cable operated by the Fuzhou Bureau of the Great Eastern Company and the Xiamen Bureau of the Great Northern Company.

Representatives of Shanghai Women's Associations Have Arrived at the Front Lines to Offer Condolences 162

Ms. Shen Huilian, Wang Xiaoying, and Wei Qiongying, representatives of the consolation group of the Chinese Women's Relief Association for Compatriots in the Northeast, traveled north by train from Nanjing on the 1st. They arrived in Peiping at noon on the 3rd and immediately contacted the Peiping Branch of the Military Commission to complete the procedures for going to the front lines. Minister He and Chief of Staff Huang (Shaoxiong) received them and sent adjutant Ji Yitian with a car to accompany them to the 29th Army's defense area to offer condolences. The army also sent Mr. Sun Yun and an adjutant to accompany them. In addition, Li Yunpeng, Chen Xiaocen, and Lie Yingjia were also traveling with them. However, Ms. Ye Jiabi and others, representatives of the women's community in Hubei, were temporarily unable to go due to illness. The group departed from Peiping at 7:00 AM on the 4th and went straight to the Zunji Highway, arriving in Jixian at 12:00 noon. Mr. Chen Zhuoru of the 29th Army's reception office provided lunch. After the meal, they continued on and arrived at the front lines of Xifengkou at 2:00 PM, where they met with Chairman Song and various division commanders. The representatives conveyed their condolences and presented condolence money and goods. Chairman Song said that the national army is responsible for defending the territory. Now that our army is holding fast to Xifengkou, it is the natural responsibility of soldiers and we dare not accept condolences. You have come all the way from Shanghai, and we are very grateful for your hard work. They were also able to view the army's war trophy room, which displayed countless enemy rifles, artillery, ammunition, iron helmets, military flags, saddles, and other items. The representatives inquired about the anti-Japanese situation and visited the battlefield, and then returned to Peiping on the same day. Because the car they came in broke down repeatedly on the way, Army Commander Song sent a car to take them back. It was heard that they arrived in Peiping at 1:00 AM in the middle of the night.

Jianghai Customs Announcement: Tax to be Levied on All Silver Bullion Exports 164

- Except for Silver Bars from the Central Mint -

Tang Haian, Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, and Bode, Tax Commissioner, issued a joint announcement No. 1290 yesterday, saying, "For the purpose of issuing a joint announcement, we have now received an order from the government stating that from April 6th of this year, with the exception of silver bars from the Central Mint, all silver ingots, silver bars, silver lumps, silver plates, and silver bullion transported overseas must be taxed at a rate of 2.25% ad valorem." We should immediately comply and hereby issue this announcement to inform all merchants. This announcement is hereby made.

The Shanghai Municipal Government assigned Secretary Zhang Tingrong to conduct a thorough review together with Bureau Director Xu Peihuang and relevant personnel. The results are as follows: (1) The hull of the No. 5 Changdu Ferry was awarded to the Hexing Machinery Manufacturing Factory. (2) The diesel engine and generator of the No. 5 Ferry were awarded to the Qianxin Machinery Company. (3) The hull of the No. 16 Duijiang Ferry was awarded to the Dachunghua Shipyard. (4) The diesel engine of the No. 16 Ferry was awarded to the Qianxin Machinery Company. (5) The chassis of the Gaoqiao public bus was awarded to the Tianxiang Foreign Company (the official chassis of the British Morris brand public bus managed by the foreign company). (6) The bus body was awarded to the Dachang Automobile Manufacturing Company. (7) The Gaoqiao bus factory was awarded to the Qiaoyuxing Construction Factory. (8) The Chunjiang Wharf ferry floating wharf and floating bridge were awarded to the Yuanda Iron Works. Contracts will be signed separately in the near future.

Resumption of Work: At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, representatives of the Fashion and Garment Workers' Union, together with the striking workers of various stores, successively entered the stores to resume work. The Situation of Shanghai Textile Mills Urgently Awaiting Improvement 170

In the past six years in Shanghai, textile mills have had the most factory fires. According to investigations, some textile mills or weaving departments have very poorly organized internal affairs, which makes them prone to fire hazards, and the risk to workers' lives is also very high after an accident. The points that urgently need attention and improvement are: (1) Many dust threads are hung on doors, windows, walls, electric lights, and all protruding or hollow places, as long as several inches, without being cleaned, and the air is full of dust, so that black clothes or female workers' hair are white. (2) The windows are filled with dust, so there is insufficient light, which leads to the opening of unnecessary lamps and candles. (3) The floor is either old or rotten, or even has holes. In the event of an accident, when the crowd runs around, one person will lose their footing, which will cause many people to fall. (4) The elevator openings for goods are not fenced off. (5) The doors to the stairwells are often locked or blocked by machines and objects. (6) In textile mills, it is necessary to increase the temperature in the air. For older factory buildings, the wooden floor may rot as a result, or it may be slippery and difficult to walk on, or the wires may be moldy due to humidity, resulting in electrical leakage. In short, due to the lack of organization of internal affairs, there are many dangerous factors. However, among the factories, there are also some with excellent order and no criticism. The dust is removed with vacuum cleaners, and the humidity is increased with new methods. The windows are wiped at any time, the machines are properly positioned, and the equipment for emergency exits is sufficient. A certain Chinese textile mill only seals the emergency exits that are not equipped for daily access with red paper strips instead of locking them, so that this door can be opened immediately in case of an accident. This method is quite imitable.

The Case of the Robbery of the Datongmen Meat Shop Was Quickly Solved 175

Patrolman Qi Bin of the First Division of the Second District Arrested the Fugitive Thief

Confessed to Using Pliers and Sugar Cakes as a Gun to Commit Robbery

Tang Sanhe Meat Shop at No. 62 Ruyi Street, Datongmen, Nanshi, is quite prosperous. At about 7:00 PM the night before last (7th), the owner of the shop, Zhu Azeng, was settling the accounts when four robbers suddenly broke into the shop. One of the robbers showed an object shaped like a gun, threatened Zhu Azeng, and threw a water tank lid on his head, forcing him to hand over silver dollars. Then, they used a meat cleaver to split open the cash counter, and a total of more than 400 yuan in paper money was robbed, and they fled in different directions. After the First District Bureau of the Public Security Bureau received the report, they immediately sent police to pursue the robbers and telegraphed to the various districts to assist in the arrest. At the same time, Patrolman Qi Bin of the First Division of the Second District of the Public Security Bureau was leading several policemen to inspect pedestrians in his jurisdiction. At about 8:00 PM, he saw a person coming at the intersection of Fuyou Road. His clothes were ragged and his expression was flustered. Patrolman Qi suspected that his behavior was suspicious and immediately ordered him to stop and checked him. He found 51 yuan in silver dollars, 49 yuan in paper money, 23 yuan in large foreign notes, 12 small silver dollars with single corners, and 320 coins with double corners in his pocket, as well as two business cards of Lu Gaosheng and Wang Boxiong. When asked where the paper money came from, he hesitated. Patrolman Qi took him to the office. The director of the office, Shen Zhenhua, repeatedly interrogated him and asked if he had robbed it from Tang Sanhe Meat Shop. He then summoned the principal, Zhu Azeng, to come to the office to testify. He confirmed that he was one of the robbers. The thief admitted that his name was Cao Jinlong, 24 years old, from Pudong. He had been in the meat shop business. Two years ago, he had made a fake gun out of sugar rice cakes at Xieqiao Xuxilu and robbed a cigarette paper shop once. This year, he had robbed a grocery store at Xinzha Bridge once. This time, he and the fugitive Amlang and others held pliers wrapped in handkerchiefs as fake guns to Tang Sanhe to threaten the principal and rob hundreds of yuan in paper money, each of which was stored in several parts, and he confessed that he would sell the stolen goods with his friends in the Xiahui Tea House in Baxianqiao. After the director of the office, Shen, according to the confession, in addition to separately ordering the police to arrest the fugitives, and sending the business cards of Lu Gaosheng and Lu Boxiong to the Detective Team for research and investigation, he had the thief Cao Jinlong, together with the stolen goods, prepared to submit a document to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for verification yesterday (8th) morning.

Old Man Froze to Death in the Spring Cold 176

The weather suddenly turned cold the night before last. An old man was frozen to death at the intersection of Xuejiabang Road, Nanshi. He was more than sixty years old and was still wearing a thin, unlined garment. The Inside Story of 25 Wooden Crates Filled with Wood Shavings and Brick Mud 177

Plan to Swap for Rayon After Customs Declaration

Three Masterminds Each Sentenced to Three Months Imprisonment

Chinese and Western detectives from the Narcotics Division of the Shanghai Municipal Police, on the 23rd of last month, searched the Wufeng Customs Brokerage at 41 Yuegui Lane, Guangdong Road, and discovered twenty-five wooden crates filled with wood shavings and brick mud, and one wooden crate of rayon. They arrested five people, including Qian Hegeng, Qi Bingwen, Zhu Miaofa, Xu Jingxiang, and Wang Heshang. They were handed over to the First Special District Court, which ordered them detained pending investigation of the purpose for which Qian and the others had prepared the wooden crates, and then questioned. This was reported in previous newspapers. Now, after a detailed investigation by the Chinese and Western detectives in charge of the case, it has been confirmed that the wooden crates were prepared by Qian, Qi, and Zhu. They learned that there were twenty-five crates of rayon worth 3,941 taels, 2 mace, and 5 candareens of silver stored at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Yangshupu. They imitated the style and made twenty-six wooden crates. Except for one crate that also contained rayon, the rest were filled with wood shavings, crushed bricks, and mud, intending to pass them off as rayon, together with the one real crate, to declare them to customs for shipment. They planned to take the opportunity to swap the crates when leaving the customs warehouse, in order to achieve their cunning plan of substituting the fake for the real. Unexpectedly, the scheme was not kept secret, and the fake goods were seized before they were shipped out. However, Xu Jingxiang and Wang Heshang did not participate in the fraudulent scheme beforehand. Yesterday morning, the police sent Qian and the other five people to the First Special Court, where Criminal Judge Feng Shide opened the court for trial. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, explained the details of the investigation. He stated that Xu and Wang had no criminal evidence and requested their release. For Qian Hegeng and the other three, they were charged with joint forgery and should be punished according to the law. Judge Feng then questioned the three defendants, Qian Hegeng, Qi Bingwen, and Zhu Miaofa, one by one. He concluded that the facts of the crime were conclusive and sentenced each of them to three months imprisonment in court. The lead sheets and other items were confiscated.

Private Red Pill Manufacturing Plant Uncovered on Rue Foch 178

They rushed to search the premises at dawn yesterday and arrested seven people, including the owner, Wang Xichen from Suzhou, the accountant, Song Liansheng, and workers Zhang Heshang, Wu Jinzhong, Xu Bingsheng, Shi Shengjin, and Zhang Asan. All of these were taken to the police station and then transferred to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District. Support Association for the Extrajudicial Killing Case in the French Concession Lodges a Serious Protest with the Municipal Government 181

-Punishment of Culprits, Apology, Etc., Have Not Been Fulfilled-

Regarding the case of the tragic deaths of two people and injuries to several others caused by extrajudicial capture in Xinqiao Street, French Concession, although several negotiations have taken place, the families of the deceased, Liu Fugao (from Ningbo) and Zhu Guding (from Chaozhou), have each been paid 2,000 yuan, and the injured have each been paid 500 yuan. However, the French Consulate has not yet fulfilled the promise of punishing the perpetrators, issuing a written apology, and guaranteeing that similar incidents will not occur in the future. Petition to the Municipal Government 182

Petition Regarding the Extrajudicial Killing Case, the French Consul's Reply is Biased, Requesting Further Serious Negotiations. The extrajudicial killing case in Xinqiao Street has aroused righteous indignation among the citizens. Therefore, an organization called the United Association to Support Tragic Cases in the French Concession was formed by various groups, and the association publicly elected Chairman Du Yuesheng of the Chinese Taxpayers' Association in the French Concession to make various demands to the French authorities. Subsequently, it was reported that the French authorities had accepted the following conditions: (1) Punish the murderers; (2) Guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future; (3) Provide compensation to the families of the deceased; (4) Provide appropriate compensation for the losses of the injured. However, because the families of the deceased had come to Shanghai from afar, they were inconvenient to stay in Shanghai for a long time, so Liu and Zhu were instructed to each receive 2,000 yuan in compensation from the French Municipal Council so that they could quickly move the coffins back to their hometowns. However, when receiving the money, it was clearly stated that although the money was received in advance, the punishment of the murderers and the guarantee must be strictly fulfilled. Chairman Du was also present at the time and reiterated this. Unexpectedly, the newspapers recently published the French Consul's reply to your government, which was infuriating to read. This must be refuted. According to eyewitnesses at the time, the extrajudicial police were arresting two women to compensate for their losses. One of the women was immediately compensated with one yuan, but she was blamed for taking a shortcut and suffering misfortune. The extrajudicial police did not understand Chinese and misunderstood the scolding, so they arrested her, forcibly dragging the woman's arm. Seeing that this was close to insulting a woman, voices of protest arose. The extrajudicial police did not sound an alarm or ask for help from other police officers, which shows that the situation was not serious at the time. Unexpectedly, he disregarded the consequences and immediately loaded his gun with live ammunition and fired two shots at the crowd. As a result, one person died to the right of the police officer, and one person died to the left of the police officer. The two injured were not in a straight line with the deceased, so who can believe it was a stray bullet? As for the claim that a number of passers-by came to attack, trying to rescue the person who violated the law, this is clearly a one-sided account of the police officer and cannot be trusted. The association believes that this matter concerns the safety and security of citizens. In addition to sending another letter to Chairman Du urging him to fulfill his promises, it is appropriate to submit a report on the facts of the case and request you to promptly order an investigation into the truth at the time, and then make a protest based on the facts, so that the murderer who intentionally killed cannot escape the death penalty, and so that the authorities can provide a written guarantee that similar incidents will not occur in the future, and issue a written apology to appease public anger and protect security. This would be a virtuous act. Respectfully submitted to Mayor Wu of the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Letter to Du Yuesheng 183

Mr. Yuesheng, I respectfully write to you. Since the tragic case in Xinqiao Street occurred, we have been extremely indignant. Based on public opinion, our association made various demands and recommended Mr. Zhang to lodge a serious protest with the French authorities. The extrajudicial police officer who intentionally killed people, and how he should be severely punished according to the law, should also be clearly announced, and cannot be left vague. This matter concerns the safety and security of citizens, and this is not enough to appease public anger and reassure the people. We hope that you will continue to work hard for the sake of millions of people, and please send the results of the negotiations to the Association as soon as possible. Respectfully yours, Shanghai Various Groups Support Association for Tragic Cases in the French Concession.

Fraudulent Fundraising Has Been Going on for Over a Year 184

Using the Name of the People's National Salvation Association

Having Raised a Total of 340 Yuan

Huang Jun and Another are Guilty of Heinous Crimes

Police Inspector Peldie (transliteration) of the French Concession Police received an anonymous letter a few days ago, stating that someone was fraudulently raising funds and extorting money in the house at No. 430 Minquan Road. Because he could not find a job and was hungry and cold, he had no choice but to commit this illegal act to make a living. He requested a clear statement. Huang also confessed that Chen Hongfa was aware of the fundraising outside, but did not share the money. Yang Zhonghe and His Heterosexual Partner 185

Cohabitation...Birth of a Daughter...Unemployment

Return Alone...Abandonment...Lawsuit

-From Union to Lawsuit-

Yang Zhonghe, from Songjiang, gave up his studies to become a businessman and came to Shanghai to work at the exchange. In 1927, Yang was already married, but his wife was in his hometown. He felt lonely while away from home and wanted to relieve his sexual frustration. He found no suitable partner in brothels. Later, a friend introduced him to a woman named Chen Xuemei. At that time, Chen was twenty years old and unmarried. Yang saw that she was beautiful, virtuous, and gentle. Affection grew daily, and in order to win her favor, he claimed that he was not yet married and wanted to spend the rest of his life with her. They cohabited for several months, and Chen became pregnant. She demanded that he fulfill his marriage promise as soon as possible to avoid being ridiculed by others. Yang initially made excuses, saying he would wait until after the birth, and then said he would communicate with his parents, using this as a pretext. Finally, because it was difficult to continue to postpone, he told Chen that he had a wife at home, and comforted her in every possible way, vowing that he would divorce

his ex-wife "Little Foreign Chicken" (the wife's name), promising a three-year period. However, by the end of 1929, Yang's exchange industry, the case wife, this place has a high cost of living, unemployed people for food, clothing, housing, self-still belong to no time, how to have the financial resources to support others, so Chen Xie gave birth to his daughter Xiao Maotou, relying on his mother's family, and he returned to Songjiang hometown, Fortunately, it is not unlearned, and it has not been idle for a long time. Later, he worked as a teacher in the county elementary school. He put Chen behind him, neither providing for him nor sending any news. Last year, Chen visited and learned that Yang had gone to Shanghai and was staying at the Far East Hotel. He took Xiao Maotou to see him, demanding support. As a result of the negotiations, Yang was willing to take Xiao Maotou home. Unexpectedly, after only one night, the next morning, he abandoned the child in the lane where Chen lived. Someone caught a glimpse and notified Chen to take her back. Until last year, Chen Xuemei felt that her youth had passed, and the girl was approaching school age. If she continued to be abandoned, not only would she be unable to make a living, but the child would also be lost. Therefore, she went to the prosecutor's office of the county court in Songjiang to file a complaint. The investigation concluded, and Yang was not prosecuted. Chen was even more disappointed. She then hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation against Yang in the First Special District Court, accusing him of abduction and abandonment. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui opened the court for trial. Chen Xuemei first described in detail how she met and cohabited with Yang Zhonghe in May 1927, through an intermediary, until everything happened. Because the defendant did not arrive, the defendant's defense lawyer claimed that the defendant was originally teaching in Songjiang, and since last year when the plaintiff filed a complaint in Songjiang, his reputation has been greatly affected. The education community in Songjiang has been unable to gain a foothold, so he has now gone to a rural elementary school in Fengxian County. He came to Shanghai specifically yesterday to entrust his lawyer to defend him, and he himself has returned to school and cannot be present in court. Judge Liu then announced that the case would be adjourned until the afternoon of April 20, and the defendant would be summoned to court for trial again.

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Offers Free Vaccinations 187

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau has been working diligently to prevent smallpox and promote free vaccinations. In addition to sending technical health personnel to large and small factories, public and private schools, and other organizations to administer vaccinations, it has also trained a large number of epidemic prevention assistants to be stationed in rural areas and provide vaccinations for rural people. Realizing that smallpox often occurs in general guest households, it has also sent personnel to work with the district chiefs and police to force vaccinations on a household-by-household basis, in order to achieve universal coverage. At the same time, it has also taken steps to prevent infectious diseases such as scarlet fever and meningitis at any time and any place, in order to avoid epidemics. The Bureau has entrusted more than 50 prevention and vaccination branches to various hospitals and universities in the city. Citizens believe that the techniques of each branch are excellent and the vaccination methods are new, and they have all gone to request vaccinations. Also, citizens who are directly vaccinated or receive other preventive vaccinations from the Bureau are also constantly coming. It is said that the number of people vaccinated against smallpox has exceeded 200,000. All our citizens who want to be vaccinated against smallpox to prevent smallpox can go directly to the Bureau or to the various prevention and vaccination branches to request vaccinations to ensure safety. The team leaders are also working hard to solicit and concentrate national salvation forces. The results of the two announcements are different and will exceed the overall goal. It is learned that the third announcement has been scheduled for 7:00 pm this evening (9th) at Jinlong Restaurant on Nanjing Road, Xizang Road. Commander-in-chief Wu and chief of staff Pan will personally attend and participate in the competition. Among the team leaders, Mr. Wu Zhihao has introduced more than 300 employees of the Shanghai National Goods Company, Mr. Qian Lijun has introduced more than 800 relatives and friends, Mr. Gu Zhuxuan has introduced more than 500 people from the community, Mr. Chen Yiting has introduced all the Shanghai cigarette factories, Mr. Sun Daosheng has introduced all the Shanghai celebrities, and Mr. Hu Xijun has introduced all the Shanghai machine factories to join as members, which is enough to show their enthusiastic competition to support the association's affairs.

Inspection Report of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank 189

The China Agricultural and Industrial Bank issued an inspection report on its issuance reserve, stating that the bank's issuance vault and business vault have always been completely separated. According to the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guarantee reserve should be below 30%. On the 8th of this month, the results of the inspection by accountant Wang Zikang and the representatives of the board of directors, Xu Jiping and Xu Busun, were as follows: Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 5,299,000 silver dollars. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 5,299,000 silver dollars, including: Cash reserve: 4,270,388 silver dollars. Guarantee reserve: 1,028,612 silver dollars. The cash reserve accounts for more than 80%, and the guarantee reserve accounts for less than 20%. This report is specially issued.

Art Mobilization Luncheon 191

Shanghai artists, in order to unite the strength of the community and cope with the national crisis, held an art mobilization luncheon at 7 pm on the 7th at the YMCA cafeteria on Sichuan Road. Attendees included Chu Huiseng, Wu Mai, and Yin Zhiling from the legal and political circles, Huang Tianzhen, Shen Yanjun, and Tang Zengyin from the press, Chen Dabei from the drama circle, Xu Xiaotian from the fiction circle, Wang Shaoqing from the film circle, Chen Gexin and Zhang Qingzhang from the music circle, Li Jinhui and Zhang Xinruo from the dance circle, Lang Jingshan from the photography circle, and Yu Yichen and Huang Shiying from the painting circle. In addition, there were Huang Jingwan and Tan Bozhi, more than 30 people in total. They gathered for lunch first, and then the temporary chairman Xu Xiaotian announced the purpose of the meeting, briefly saying that in today's serious national crisis, it is necessary to mobilize the masses. To awaken the national salvation spirit of the masses, it is necessary to use the most stimulating art, and the art world must implement total mobilization first. Today's meeting is to unite art seniors and social celebrities to jointly organize an art and national salvation group, in order to achieve our mission in the shortest time. This is the national duty, and I hope you will give your advice. Then Wu Mai and Zhu Huiseng stood up to supplement their opinions, mainly saying that Chinese people's organizations are often all show and no substance. Today, it is a matter of course to unite the art world to save the country together, but at the beginning of the initiation, we must first have the spirit of sacrifice. If you think that this organization is not needed, you can disband it immediately. Otherwise, you must persevere to the end and strive for success. National destruction is imminent, and there is no room for superficiality. At that time, it was passed that all attendees would join as initiators. In addition, Zhu Huiseng, Wu Mai, Xu Xiaotian, Chen Dabei, Huang Jingwan, Yu Yichen, and Shen Yanjun were elected as preparatory committee members to prepare the draft of the articles of association and the task of convening the inaugural meeting. Xu Xiaotian was appointed as the convener. By the time the meeting adjourned, the clock had struck ten. It is said that the office of the organization is temporarily located in Qingniao Club, 1152 Jing'an Temple Road, telephone number 35562.

Medical World 194

New Treatment for Meningitis: Meningitis, known as "epidemic spasm" in Chinese medicine, is gradually becoming popular in Shanghai, and is especially rampant in Wuhu. Deaths are successive, which is truly pitiable. Now, the Chinese Medicine Guidance Society, after three years of research and experimentation, has published the following opinions: (Symptoms) In the early stage, there are symptoms of cold and fever, headache like splitting, numbness in the limbs, irritability, nausea, with or without sweating. As it worsens, there are stiff neck and convulsions, opisthotonos, unclear consciousness, red and staring eyes, lockjaw and delirium. Finally, the stiff neck and opisthotonos worsen, the lips are scorched and the tongue is black, or the limbs are cold, or there is manic restlessness, or phlegm rattles and shortness of breath, or red spots are visible, or the mouth is full of erosion. (Causes) The weather is often cold and hot, and the air is turbid, brewing into an epidemic. In the early stage, it may be accompanied by cold or warmth, and over time, it stagnates and turns into heat, going up the spine and entering the brain. (Treatment) In the early stage, Gegen Tang is the main prescription, with additions and subtractions according to symptoms to relieve the symptoms. As it worsens, Lingyang and Xijiao are the main medicines, with additions and subtractions according to symptoms to clear and drain the heat. For emergency rescue, Zixue, Zhibao, and Niuhuang Xingjun Yushu pills are the main agents, used according to symptoms. The aftermath is mainly to clear the camp and support yin, and treated according to symptoms. (Formulas) Qin's Antispasmodic and Antitoxin Decoction is suitable for the early stage of epidemic spasm, with symptoms such as aversion to cold and fever. Gegen, mulberry leaves, and white peony each two qian, Chrysanthemum, Trichosanthes, Forsythia, and apricot kernels each three qian, ephedra and cinnamon each eight fen, Ledebouriella root one and a half qian. If sweating is excessive, remove ephedra. If internal heat is heavy, add one liang of reed root. Qin's Detoxifying Decoction for Epidemic Spasm is suitable for the advanced stage of epidemic spasm, with severe heat, coma, and opisthotonos. Antelope horn and yellow su each five fen, white peony and Ren Zhong Huang each two qian, Acorus tatarinowii one and a half qian, honeysuckle, Forsythia, Trichosanthes, Chrysanthemum each three qian, oyster shell and reed root each one liang. If the heat is heavy, add three fen of rhinoceros horn. If constipation, add three qian of rhubarb. If body fluid is dry, add four qian of Rehmannia glutinosa. (Note: The society is located at No. 194, Shangwen Road, inside Xiaoximen, Shanghai. The director is Mr. Qin Bowei. For any unclear points, you can directly inquire by letter, which is also good news during the epidemic).

Miscellaneous News 195

Yu Youren Praises Zhu Tiezhi's Seal Carving: Zhu Tiezhi of Yun Jian is skilled in appraisal and loves seal carving. His seal carving has a profound taste, entering the Zhejiang and Anhui schools from the Qin and Han dynasties. He uses the knife like a pen, rounding smoothly, so his works are full of ancient charm and are valued by scholars. Wu Changshuo once set a price list for him. Later, due to busy party and government affairs, those who sought his work often had regrets. Those who obtained even a fragment of stone or a single character regarded it as a treasure and were extremely precious. Now, Mr. Zhu has put aside external affairs and specializes in iron brushes to benefit fellow enthusiasts. Mr. Yu Youren and others specially recommend him, so that those who love epigraphy can inquire. Collection points: Author's Bookstore on Fourth Malu, Shanghai, and major bookstores and fan shops.

Inheriting his family's learning, he has refined the study of Taijiquan, Taiji sword, and Taiji spear, all of which have a reputation for being unique. Although Mr. Wu is over sixty years old, he is still energetic. He teaches students with great care and is strict but not harsh, explaining the meaning and usage without any ambiguity. His disciples are all over the provinces. Internal family boxing can be learned by people of all ages, strengths, and weaknesses. It can not only strengthen the body but also cure diseases. Therefore, many celebrities and large companies in Shanghai hire Mr. Wu as a teacher, and many people come to learn. His residence is at No. 5, Taoyuan Village, Lafayette Road, French Concession.

Reader's Advisor

A Collection of Letters Discussing the Question "Can We Go Back to the Countryside?" 200

(1) Letter from Mr. Shiyu of this city

I am now a small clerk in a company. Because of the threat of unemployment, I am thinking of going to the countryside like Mr. Xiongsheng. Mr. Xiongsheng's situation, with an old mother above and a wife below, makes it very difficult to find another job in the city after being unemployed, which is almost the same as my situation. Therefore, when I saw that you designed a way for Mr. Xiongsheng to return to the countryside, I was very happy, and I could follow it in the future. However, after reading your method, dark shadows still surround me. Not only is it that the lofty aspirations of "a leader standing out from the crowd" cannot inspire me, but it also shatters my fantasy of "returning to my hometown may allow me to earn a bowl of rice." According to the editor's introduction, you are an enthusiastic advocate of rural education to save the country, have a lot of research on rural education, and are also a practitioner. It seems that your views will not be wrong. Now I will write down the places where I feel disappointed with your method one by one, and ask you to explain and correct them. If you can really guide us to open up a way to survive, Mr. You, there are many young people like me and Xiongsheng in today's society, and they will be very grateful to you. (1) I cannot manage to raise one or two hundred yuan from relatives and friends in your first step. One or two hundred yuan may seem like a small amount to you, Mr. You, but it is a very large sum of money in the eyes of us poor scholars. Moreover, in such a "cold and worldly" society, let alone the fact that most people do not have wealthy relatives and friends, even if they do, they will take it to lend at interest or do something profitable for them. Who would be willing to use it to help those of us who have no way to make a living? You, Mr. You, tell us to raise money, but you don't give us a plan to repay the debt. Who would give one or two hundred yuan out of thin air? (2) Mr. Xiongsheng and I both have old mothers and wives. Your design only takes into account one person. We are not incapable of using extremely frugal methods to solve life. Waste is not associated with the poor, but rather with the inability to obtain the minimum living materials. Old mothers and wives cannot be abandoned to starve to death. Not being able to find a job means that food and shelter cannot be solved, let alone talking about what kind of clothes to wear in summer and what kind of robes to wear in winter. (3) Even if there are no above two difficulties, no burden of family members, and you can find generous relatives and friends like Mr. You, willing to lend us one or two hundred yuan, isn't it simply giving us one or two hundred yuan, can we solve personal life and lead the masses, save China? We will divide it into three sections to discuss. (1) As for the question of personal life, if we are as frugal as Mr. You instructed, one or two hundred yuan can indeed be spent in the countryside for two or three years. However, when it comes to running a school to maintain a permanent life, the problem is not that simple. Why is rural education in China so backward? Is it because intellectuals don't care to go to the countryside? Or is it that the countryside doesn't want intellectuals to set foot in it? According to Mr. You, the prerequisite for going to the countryside is something like "Do you love the countryside?" Naturally, intellectuals are unwilling to go to the countryside. I don't know what Mr. You's hometown is like, but my hometown doesn't want intellectuals. First, under the economic invasion of imperialism, my hometown went bankrupt. Because of the constant warlord wars that have resulted from the conflict between imperialism, rural economy has been extremely destroyed. Under the oppression and exploitation of disasters, wars, harsh taxes, and high interest rates, the peasants cannot even get enough to eat all year round. Where can they spare any effort to take care of their children's education? No matter how much sacrificial spirit we hold, without charging tuition, stationery, paper, books, etc., they are already overwhelmed. What's more, they have to pay a chicken, or a duck, or thirty eggs. Moreover, when children in the countryside reach school age, they are not as idle as children in the city. When they are five or six years old, they can go grazing, chopping wood, and doing all kinds of light work. Those poor and hardworking peasants don't have the same thoughts as Mr. You, telling them to sacrifice helpful children to read books that "cannot be eaten when hungry or worn when cold" is indeed a bit impossible. Second, of course, not all peasants in the countryside are completely destitute. Although wealthy landlords have run to the city, there are also middle peasants who can barely afford to provide their children with a little education. However, we must know that their future is very dark, and they are gradually moving towards destitution. Placing our career on these people, hoping to rely on these people to maintain our personal life, will inevitably lead to starvation. Third, we know that the road Mr. You is talking about is not one that no one has taken. Many previous scholars have already gone there long ago. Even in Guizhou, the province with the most backward culture, there are bound to be two or three private schools in a village where only ten farmers live. If you go to a market town with hundreds of people, there will be some small schools with signs. The countryside is withering day by day, and the population is gradually moving to the city. Under extreme poverty, does the countryside still have the power to absorb us, the intellectual class who have no way to make a living? Mr. You, do you have anything to tell me? (2) As to whether Mr. Xiongsheng can be a good leader in the countryside, I don't know Mr. Xiongsheng, but according to Xiongsheng himself, he is very humble, just a person who has no special skills and can only write a few words. I am indeed just a person with no special skills. Do Mr. You and Mr. Xiongsheng know each other? I think it's probably not. If Mr. Xiongsheng had known Mr. You earlier, he must have been guided by Mr. You to go to the countryside. Why would he still write a letter asking the reader advisor column's reporter to solve his own problems? So how does Mr. You know that Mr. Xiongsheng can be a leader in the countryside? If anyone who can write can be a leader in the countryside, can I do it too? Can those scholars of the previous dynasty do it too? Mr. You, you are a person who advocates rural education. What conditions do you think a rural teacher should have? What do we take to teach children in the countryside? How do we lead those peasants under double oppression? (3) As for the question of whether rural education can save the country, I am not an educator and I don't understand. However, I always feel that the organization of society is fundamentally based on economics. If there is no way to solve the economy, politics will be chaotic. Under a poor economy and chaotic politics, all construction is empty talk, all deception, and cultural undertakings are no exception. And to have hope for China's economic future, sweeping away imperialism and all its parasitic forces is the only prerequisite? Everything else is nonsense. However, Mr. You thinks that rural education can save the country. Because I trust the editor's introduction, I also want to listen to your high views. In short, can we really go back to the countryside in China now? Can the countryside be revived? Can rural education really save China? Is it the only way out for Chinese youth to take on rural education? Please give me an answer, Mr. You. As for the issues of running cooperatives and conducting village governance, I would like to leave it to those who have studied it to discuss. I will not get involved.

Page 20

Spring and Autumn

Tang Erhu 201

— Zhan Lu

A businessman who returned from Shenyang felt extremely saddened by the fall of Chengde, believing that it had let down the hopes of the 30 million people outside the pass!

The people outside the pass, especially the merchants, were all eagerly awaiting good news from the war. They believed that the enemy had declared their attack on Rehe for over a year. They thought that young commander Zhang would hold the resentment of "not living under the same sky as the killer of his father," and Tang Erhu, who was defending Rehe, was a man of bravery and spirit, of whom the old commander was afraid by three points even in his lifetime. With thorough deployments, how could the enemy easily invade? There was even hope of recovering Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang. Who knew that before long, Japanese newspapers had already widely reported the victory in the invasion of Rehe: that a small team of over a hundred men easily captured Chengde, and that only one person died and two were injured in the attack on Gubeikou. They all shook their heads in disbelief, thinking that it was a false propaganda by the Japanese. Taking advantage of Mr. So-and-so's return home, they entrusted him to find out the truth about the war and report it to them, so that they could dispel their doubts.

After Mr. So-and-so returned, the facts told him that they were speaking with the same tongue as the propaganda in the Japanese newspapers! Tang Erhu had fled! Young commander Zhang had gone south! Such inauspicious news, if written in a letter to inform the compatriots outside the pass, wouldn't it close the door of their hope? Wouldn't it open the floodgates of their tears?

Whether young commander Zhang will avenge himself or not? Let's put that aside for now and wait for the next installment. Some people say that this Tang Erhu, who was always known for his bravery and who the old commander was afraid of by three points, has inevitably tainted the fine name of "Erhu." It is commonly said that someone with abundant strength is called "nine oxen and two tigers." Does he deserve to be called "Erhu?" It would be better to call him "One Crab"; he fled before the enemy even reached the city, and compared to other fleeing generals, he can be said to be "one crab is worse than another." It would be better to call him "One Duck"; his anti-Japanese telegram was so generous and tragic. It fits the saying "a duck in a soup pot, only the mouth comes out." Moreover, his desertion has already been confirmed, and he has also sent a telegram saying that he wants to take back Chengde, so it can be seen that his duck mouth is still not softened. Calling him "Tang One Duck" is more consistent with his name and reality.

Some people say: Tang Erhu is a tiger internally, not externally. He is indeed a tiger who eats people without spitting out bones to the common people, but towards the dwarf tiger, he becomes not a tiger but a "rat" that flees with its head in its hands. According to this, he can also be called Tang One Rat.

Restoration 202

— Bai He

Being an emperor is the noblest and most enjoyable profession in the world. Within a country, one is supreme, able to do as one pleases. If the emperor says that farts are fragrant, who would dare wrinkle their nose and frown. Because being an emperor is simply the most comfortable thing, even dogs and cats, Da Liuzi and Xiao Sanzi, although possessing a demeanor unfit for such a position, would still claim to have the appearance of an emperor in their death throes, dreaming of the imperial throne. However, I, observing the situation, feel that in this current era, being an emperor is not very enjoyable. Today, one may be solemnly receiving the congratulations of thousands of subjects, but in the middle of the night, a revolution erupts, and before dawn, one might be dragged out of a warm bed by revolutionaries and exiled to a deserted island.

The emperor who has broken his imperial rice bowl does not suffer the pain of being cut in two or beheaded to be displayed to the public, but merely lives in exile on a deserted island or lives in hiding in a foreign country. This is because his five elements and eight characters are good, at least he has a Violet Emperor star shining on his life, so breaking his imperial rice bowl is only a temporary period of hiding his light and nourishing his strength. One day, a trapped dragon gains water, and can still stir up wind and waves, make a comeback, and regain the dragon throne, calling himself lonely.

It is said that everything in the world cannot escape the cycle of creation, the circle of heaven and earth, yin and yang. When Tai reaches its extreme, there is obstruction, and when obstruction reaches its extreme, there is Tai. People are always tumbling in this. The political trends of various countries are also like this. When autocratic politics reaches its peak, it inevitably comes down to democratic politics. Democratic politics expand into a swelling disease, leading to a system of socialism. When the socialist system becomes a semi-paralyzed person, then "you are bad, overthrow you, I will do it," the stage turns, the supporting actors come on stage, the deposed emperor is restored, and a scene of dictatorial politics is staged. Thus, the emperor, who has been unemployed for a long time, finds his imperial rice bowl again. Although it is not certain whether this newly arranged restoration comedy will sell out or be booed by the audience, keeping an actor with the appearance of an emperor and a Violet Emperor star shining on his life will inevitably itch for a genuine show.

Spring Arrives in the Countryside 204

— Xu Mu Xi

The spring maiden has finally bashfully arrived in Jiangnan. The serene countryside is adorned with nature's beauty, so the red flowers bloom as usual, and the birds sing actively on the branches. The gentlemen and young ladies in the city, attracted by the universe's love and nurture, shout, "Spring has arrived! It's time for picnics! Let's have a picnic!" Oh, you leisurely people! We don't need you to come.

Are you coming to seek amusement from the songs of field poets? Are you coming to breathe fresh air after being tired of city life for so long? Go away! The countryside has been hurt by you. From now on, we will never let the stench of capitalism rush into the countryside again!

Pitifully, we don't have a single silver dollar on us. Pitifully, our accumulated hard work has only earned us broken scars. It is you who have absorbed our money, it is you who have exported our money overseas! And you still want to talk about going to the countryside? There are no suits and leather shoes in the countryside! Look! Our plain clothes and simple meals!

You only know how to enjoy yourselves, you don't know the hardships of the world. When you see a fisherman fishing by the stream, you say, "What a quiet and meaningful game!" Do you know that one day's harvest is not enough to feed a family? Enough! You always come to destroy our countryside, go away! People full of the stench of capitalism.

We have our own gardens, our green hills and clear waters belong to the public, our field life is communal, our spring is beautiful, but we absolutely don't need you to transform it. The countryside is fundamentally primitive!

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 205

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Four: The Affair Rekindles at the Teahouse, Accumulated Feelings; the Year-End is Hard to Get Through, the Pawnshop Laments

When Jiang received that big bowl of stewed beef from the Zhao family that day, she felt a great stimulation in her heart. She thought to herself, if my child were a son, wouldn't he be just like this, able to stew a big bowl of beef for me to eat? But then she thought, there are many people in the world who rely on their sons to support them in old age, but how many sons who support them are able to stew beef for their parents? There are two old people on this street who rely on their sons, but the sons all wear good clothes and eat good food, while the old people are pitifully poor. So it seems that saying that having a son means having someone to rely on in old age is not very reliable. It's really unnecessary to have a son like Zhao Company Commander. Even having a son-in-law like him would be satisfying. I think the Zhao father and son are so kind and thoughtful to my family, could it be that they want to propose marriage to my family? And judging from my daughter's attitude, she has always looked down on soldiers, but she always says good things about this Zhao Company Commander, whether in person or behind his back. Could it be that this child has Zhao Company Commander in her heart? As she thought this, she felt it was more and more likely. Taking this opportunity to settle her daughter's lifelong affair would also be the responsibility of a parent. Having made up her mind, that evening, she sat on the kang with Guizhi, sharing a kerosene lamp while sewing clothes. The mother and daughter chatted idly, and Guizhi asked again if the beef was delicious. Jiang lowered her head and kept holding the clothes in her hand, threading the needle and sewing busily. She seemed to be paying little attention to her daughter, casually replying: How could it not be delicious? How many times a year does our family get to eat it? Guizhi said: That's what I thought too. Our family doesn't have days when we eat meat, so when Old Master Zhao sent it to me, I didn't refuse and brought it back. Jiang said: Yes! The old master saw that our family was poor, so he sent us this bowl of beef. Both he and his son have good hearts. As she said this, she raised her head slightly, her eyes hidden behind her glasses, and glanced at Guizhi. Seeing that Guizhi was still calmly sewing clothes, she added: Zhao Company Commander is an even better person.

Being a company commander, I wonder how much money he can earn in a month! (36)

Foot Massage 206

— Yu Qing

Having a foot massage in a bathhouse has a special flavor. Wrapped in a large towel or bathrobe, you lie back on the kang bed, stretching your feet straight out, placing them on the knees of the foot massager sitting on a low stool. You close your eyes and concentrate, or smoke a cigarette, letting him massage your feet. If the massage is neither itchy nor painful, but instead makes your soles feel a little itchy, then you must slightly raise your head and gently say to the foot massager: "Harder!" The foot massager uses a little more force, and this wave of pleasure makes you "float like an immortal rising to heaven." At this moment, your eyes will become hazy, and perhaps the corners of your mouth will automatically stretch to the sides of your face, indicating that you are currently experiencing this wave of numbness and tasting a part of the pleasure of the flesh. However, once this wave of pleasure passes, I'm sorry, your soles have been massaged until the skin is broken, and you feel pain in your soles. You suffer this pain, it's self-inflicted; you can't get angry and blame the foot massager for being too heavy-handed. You can only raise your head slightly for the second time, put on a "that's enough" expression, and gently say to the foot massager: "That's enough!" Seeing that your soles are broken and bloody, with traces of blood seeping into the broken towel, the foot massager immediately sprinkles powder to cover it up, without saying anything else.

Recently, Yosuke Matsuoka, the chief representative of Japan at the League of Nations, gave a speech to Japanese expatriates during his trip to Chicago, saying these two sentences: "We will use force only when necessary." All 400 million compatriots in China, please look! That's all there is to it, without saying anything else.

Children's Paradise

In Praise of Children 207

— Ding Ming

"Children," "Children," what a fragrant, sweet, and tenderly soft pleasing noun this is! Children, children, what a group of energetic activists full of enthusiasm, brightness, and upward spirit!

From a broader perspective! Children are the future masters of the country, the central point of cultural transmission, and also the pivotal point for transitioning from the current century to the utopian and blissful century of the future.

To use an analogy; Children are like sparkling stars in the night, and also like dazzling lightning illuminating the globe. They are like softly flowing water flowing eastward, and also like tender buds of vegetation sprouting. They are like flower buds, and also like angels in imagination 丨丨丨 little angels.

Children are the sparkling sparks in everyone's life, the heart and soul of everyone, an invisible stimulant in everyone's life, and also an element in everyone's life, a living treasure and a lifeline for everyone. They are also the lively masters with sound, color, and form among mankind; without children, there would be no world. Children are the only comforters of people's souls, without children, it would be tantamount to declaring one's own life a death sentence, like those intellectual celibates, the virgins, who are themselves executing themselves as representatives of prisoners serving "life imprisonment."

The current physical health of children is a symbol of the future physical health of adults; the current mental health of children is an omen of the future soundness of knowledge, ethnicity, and career.

The hearts of children are more pure than snowflakes, they are the purest; without the hypocrisy, cunning, and exaggeration of adults, stained with heavy pigments; almost stained beyond recognition, burying their own childlike innocence and losing their original appearance.

Children are uncrowned emperors, jumping and leaping, talking and laughing, crying and yelling, very free and very equal. The actions of children are very natural! Very grand! Very beautiful! When they are hungry, they cry out loud; when they are full, they fart and shit regardless of whether they are in public or before a king, unlike adults who say human words in front of people and ghost words behind their backs.

They can't reach the magpie's nest in the tree branches, but they insist on trying. They climb with both hands and feet like monkeys. After only a few feet, they fall down, but children have a determined spirit of perseverance! One day, two days, they finally climb up!

Children are the most content, the most adventurous, and the most fearless; "Good boy! Fire! Fire! Fire! Fire!" He doesn't believe it, he touches it with his finger and cries! From then on, he dares not again! Afterwards, he increases his belief in the words of adults!

The life of childhood is the happiest life in life. When they are happy, they roll and roll, walk and walk, run and run, jump and jump; when they are tired, they not only sleep in a cradle, but also lie in their mother's arms. When they grow up, they fly kites in the spring, go to the park in the summer, tread on fragrant grass and play games, or flutter through the woods like butterflies; they fish in the autumn, chase chickens, or lie in a pile of sorghum stalks and bask in the sun; they huddle around the stove for warmth at home in the winter.

However, children with faces full of mud, hawking along the streets, are children; children being beaten by their uncles, scolded by their aunts, and laughed at by their siblings are also children. Children with ragged clothes and thin bones are children, children who are illiterate and dull-witted are children; children who are lifeless during festivals are children, children with eccentric personalities and strange behaviors are also children; children who cry without tears when they see people and reach out their hands when they meet people are children, children who are hopping on one foot, bending over, jumping like dogs, and dancing like monkeys are also children; children who are barefoot and sweating under the scorching sun in the city in the summer, shouting, "It's cool! Buy ice!" are children; children who are carrying broken baskets to pick up dry branches in the winter are also children, children in the countryside who carry a small shovel on a long pole, driving a flock of sheep up the mountains to greet the sunrise and send off the sunset, are children, children who are chattering their teeth and shivering, sifting blue coal (second-generation coal) in the sand like panning for gold are also children. Children! Children! There are all kinds of good things, and also all kinds of bad things; there are all kinds of luck, and also all kinds of bad luck. It is the fault of the parents, and also the crime of society; it is the poison of feudal inheritance, and even more so the unending responsibility of today's intellectuals and those who hold political authority.
