Free Talk

Political Power and Civil Rights 208

— Yu Lianfu

Recently, the newspapers have been clamoring about a speech by an old Kuomintang comrade who has been traveling north and south, saying that the government has made a firm decision to open up political power. ?

To open up political power, as guessed by us ordinary people who have never tasted the taste of political power, probably means that everyone shares the food and everyone becomes an official. From now on, there will be peace in the world, and everyone will have a future. You don't have to fight, and I don't have to make a fuss. We will gather together in harmony, hang up the national flag, and put on our belts. Poets must prepare to become poetry officials, and novelists will have to become minor officials. It is said that the women of Peiping have already caught up and become female patrol officers. In this way, everyone becomes an official, and externally, we will jointly face national difficulties, and internally, we will prepare for constitutionalism - these four characters also caused a sensation during the Guangxu reign of the Manchu Qing Dynasty - steam my hair, bind you with a good title, heroes of the world, enter my snare, wouldn't that be grand, wouldn't that be delightful.

But upon careful thought, we have 400 million compatriots. No matter how much you increase the number of committee members and parliamentarians, it probably won't accommodate 400 million black-hatted officials. Moreover, the capable are burdened with more work, and those who are close to the people must at least concurrently hold seventeen or eighteen prominent positions. The yamen is wide open, the constitution is written on paper, calling a beggar to play the role of a spring official, a dream of Handan, and the two hundred big boards that follow are truly unbearable. Therefore, we poor bones who are used to being poor should consolidate our civil rights as soon as possible, which is more practical.

I think that if political power is to be opened up, why should civil rights be so closed off? A copy of Ma's Grammar can actually be used as evidence of endangering the Republic of China, and a novel lamenting poverty can even constitute a death sentence for a journalist. In addition, there are countless other political suspects who don't eat mutton and have a slightly muttony smell. Even a memorial gathering for deceased sages must be reported early and can only be implemented after approval. There are truly many such facts, too many to remember. I think that if political power is to be opened up, why must civil rights be so tightly closed off?

Sanfu the Tailor 209

— Peng Xuezhen

Outside it was cold wind, cold rain, cold air. Inside the house it was gloomy, the weak light of a small oil lamp trembled in the dark. Sanfu lay on the bedding stuffed with straw, coughing and panting, his forehead covered in sweat, his face oily, and messy black stubble around his mouth, his small eyes squeezed even smaller by his tightly furrowed brows.

Although he was already forty-six or forty-seven years old, this was the first time in his life that he had been sick in bed for three or four days. He knew how to "endure", refusing to lie down until he really couldn't hold on any longer; this time, he really couldn't control himself. Although at first he adopted a "let it go" attitude and endured for a day or two, in the end he finally lay down.

From the age of eight or nine, he had been taking needles and thread in a tailor shop as an apprentice, and he didn't know how many times he had eaten shoe soles (been bullied), leaving a scar more than an inch long on his forehead to this day. Because of this, after Sanfu finally managed to become the shopkeeper, he never beat his apprentices.

Although he became the shopkeeper, Sanfu's hard and poor fate didn't change much. And because he started a family, the heavy burden of life pressed him down even more.

The year before last was even more unlucky, when his wife unexpectedly died, leaving him with a daughter who wasn't even a month old in addition to two boys, one eight and one nine years old. Sanfu was so heartbroken that he had no tears, just staring at the sky in a daze. The coffin bill wasn't paid off until the Mid-Autumn Festival last year, and he almost got beaten by the bill collector.

After his wife died, Sanfu's life seemed to have lost its purpose, and he had no energy for anything. But when he thought of the children his wife had left behind, he could only sew even more diligently and run even more diligently on the streets.

Although there were many people who wanted Sanfu to make clothes, it was really hard to bear the expressions on their faces when he stretched out his hand to ask for payment once the clothes were made! Although the price he charged was fairer than other tailors, people always glared at him: "Come and get it at the festival, I won't cheat you!" But when it came time to collect the money at the festival, they would say: "Come and get it next festival, will I run away?"

Although the customers' wages were always delayed, the wages of the workers couldn't be delayed. Every month, Sanfu didn't know how many nice things he had to say and how much thought he had to put in to get by. When it came to days when they ate meat, he never forgot to buy half a catty more meat to treat the workers, so that everyone would be more energetic.

What he feared most was the finger-numbing winter, when the work was particularly slow, but the people who wore the clothes couldn't wait to have them today if they were cut tomorrow. Sanfu had heard enough of the customers' fierce instructions, so he repeatedly begged Old Wang and Old Li to work overtime, offering three cents when they wouldn't agree for two, and he himself accompanied them, sewing even harder. But when he finished and delivered the clothes, the customer still said that they were made too coarsely and that he would get the money at the end of the year. Sanfu could only complain; I sewed these with sleepy eyes!

At this time, the sound of two children snoring filled the house. He remembered: Didn't Dabao clamor for a new robe yesterday? People laughed at Dabao, how come his dad is a tailor and he still doesn't dress neatly? Yes, he just can't save another dollar this month. Erbao had to pay some fees, saying that there would be a meeting tomorrow to buy snacks, and last night he begged Erbao; "Good boy, can you not go to school tomorrow?" Erbao cried for half an hour clutching his quilt for this reason. Xiaomao's breastfeeding money was also being forced to be paid, three dollars a month, enough to bear!

Now he himself had fallen ill, unable to work and still having to spend money to see a doctor and buy medicine. Who could he blame? He was too presumptuous, working for three days and nights without taking a nap to rush Old Grandpa Qin's shroud, and he got sick before he got the money. Coughing, wheezing, unable to move his waist and back, feeling pain as if he was clamping a bullet, his shoulders always aching as if they were about to break. But, in this deep night, he didn't dare to groan loudly, fearing that he would wake the workers from their good sleep and they wouldn't be able to work tomorrow.

Sanfu was tired, panting softly, calculating in a daze the rice and firewood for tomorrow, Dabao's new jacket, Erbao's two-cent fee...

When will this bitter fate end!

Tolstoy on Women 210

— Shi Jingxie

Among many literary figures, Tolstoy can be considered one of the most frequent to mention women. Whether in essays, in plays or novels, he always used a stern and cold attitude to criticize the current social system, and used a generous tone to defend innocent women. In "Kreutzer Sonata" he said: "······Those coercive means (coercive means to cure syphilis) are not used to eliminate lust but to encourage lust; guaranteeing that lust is not dangerous, what is that? Almost no one does not encounter that terrible thing, not to mention young people, I am afraid that nine out of ten have suffered this pain, even the farmers in the countryside cannot be spared. The reason for this is not because women have bewitching means, women will never bewitch people; it is because some people regard lust as legal, beneficial to health, and some people regard it as a most natural and not at all sinful game for young people.······

In fact, Tolstoy, in daily conversation, would utter a torrent of wonderful theories about women as soon as he discussed them. Once he met Gorky and talked about women's chastity, taking the short story "Twenty-Six Men and a Girl" written by Gorky as the topic. Tolstoy said: "Chastity"? This is certainly unnatural for ladies who are healthy and fully developed. Women over the age of fifteen, if she is healthy and fully developed, then she must be very happy to be touched and embraced by the opposite sex in her heart! However, on the other hand, she is very worried in her mind about something she does not understand and has not experienced: the concept of so-called "chastity," "purity," and "flawlessness" lies in this point. However, no matter how worried she is in her heart, her flesh always thinks that this thing she has not fully understood is a legitimate and legal behavior, so she constantly asks her to fulfill this law!"

Once, when he was walking with Chekhov, he suddenly opened his mouth and asked Chekhov: "Hey! Old brother! You must have had a lot of fun whoring when you were young!" Chekhov did not answer, but chuckled with a wry smile. Tolstoy looked at the sea again, as if lost in thought, and said: "In fact, I also like women very much and never get tired of them!" On another occasion, Gorky, Chekhov, and others were talking about women, and Tolstoy sat beside them listening attentively for a long time before he opened his mouth and said: "The truth about women? I'll tell you when one of my feet steps into the grave! At that time, after I say it, I want to jump into the coffin immediately, hurriedly put the coffin lid on, and then shout: "Hey! Do as you please!"

Linlin 211

— Ba Rong

Some people say that childhood is a golden age, it is like a rose in spring, in full bloom, it flourishes in gentle love, it does not know what is called sadness in the world!

But our Linlin is completely different, he was born and grew up in pain, his father is a street sweeper, his mother is a disabled woman!

When he was ten years old, he was oppressed by life, spending his youth in a dark factory, working all day long without stopping, and the reward he got was only cold and hunger!

It was in this environment that he gradually grew up, the factory turned him into iron bones and copper tendons, and his tenacious character was also formed here, he constantly uttered angry cries!

He understood that to live, he could only struggle, and only a strong team could have a strong force. He called on the masses to rise from hell! But alas, he finally went to the "slaughterhouse"!

Now, although his body has become dust, his name is still engraved in the hearts of some people! He grew up in sorrow and pain! He died in a tragic war!

Long Creative Writing

The Crossroads of the Times and Love 212

— Zhang Ziping

So people imagine those ferocious imperialist lackeys - the informers and patrolmen of the concession, beasts who specialize in sucking the blood of compatriots. In addition, there are foreign beasts, especially the patrolmen in the Hongkou area, strutting along North Sichuan Road, grinning at the Chinese with ashen faces on both sides of the road. Although he hated them, he was also afraid of them. The day before yesterday, in the branch, a comrade gave such an impassioned speech, saying that rather than being slowly slaughtered to death by them, those imperialists, it would be better to fight them and their lackeys to the death one day sooner, which would be more enjoyable. Individual life originally has little meaning. Our comrades must fight for society, and fight for the lives of the broad masses of poor people. There is no meaning in sitting in a pavilion reading socialist books and writing socialist articles. We need action, - we need revolutionary action!

At that time, Haiquan's enthusiasm was indeed stirred up by the speech of this committee member, and he applauded with the crowd, and he wanted to immediately go to the forefront of anti-imperialism.

Later, a vote was taken to participate in the demonstration parade, and it was unanimously approved. But after the meeting, when he came out and was blown by the cold wind on the street, Haiquan's enthusiasm disappeared to who knows where.

"This is an adventure! A very dangerous adventure!"

So he thought of Mrs. Tsuruko again, thought of Peizhu, thought of Zhuo Shuhua, and even thought of Mrs. Cao Shiguang, and then thought of his old grandmother and parents living in the southern countryside. From his parents at home, he thought of the money that had not yet been remitted home.

"Do it! Go forward bravely and do it! A good Chinese man should not be so cowardly! This is the work that Chinese youth cannot shirk - the work of liberating the Chinese nation, and the work of finding a way out for the broad masses of poor people"!

He was daydreaming while holding this letter. He imagined the scene when he was pulled into the police station by the patrol. He also remembered the pain in prison that the advanced people who had lived in the Western prison had told him about. He was a little scared again.

"Mr. Lin, where did the letter come from, you're reading it with such enthusiasm, is it a love letter"?

Qiuying walked forward holding a child, smiling at him. Her face was almost leaning on one of his arms. He smelled a fragrance again. For a long time, he didn't open his mouth, just glanced at her quickly and couldn't help but smile.

"Can I see it?"

She asked him with a red face and a smile.

"You can't understand it".

He smiled and tucked the letter into his pocket.

American Cotton Review of the Past Week 227

Counterparts Have Been Absorbing, While Southern Selling is Extremely Rare

More than a thousand Chinese were temporarily hired at four corners each, and many suffered the same tragic fate. (9th dispatch)

After this defeat, the "Manchu" army advancing towards Qinhuangdao was also forced to retreat. At the same time, the Chinese army has quickly arrived in Qinhuangdao. (9th dispatch)

Tranquility on the Gubekou Front, Only Minor Contact at the Outposts 239

(Beiping) War reports from Gubekou have been relatively quiet in recent days. There have only been outpost battles. The majority of the enemy troops are concentrated in Qian, planning to launch a large-scale flanking attack on the Lengkou Tanghe line, with the puppet troops as the vanguard and the Japanese army supervising from behind. (9th dispatch)

Han Linjun, Member of the First Central Committee, Has Been Released on Bail 240

(Beiping) Han Linjun, a member of the first Central Committee of the Kuomintang who was expelled for his connection to the Communist Party, was arrested in Tianjin a few years ago. He was recently strongly vouched for by Sun Dianying, who also guaranteed that Han would have absolutely no connection with the Communist Party from now on and would wholeheartedly serve the Party and the country. The Central Government, considering Sun's strong request, has now restored Han's freedom. (9th dispatch)

Xu Yongchang Arrives in Beiping 241

(Beiping) Xu Yongchang arrived in Beiping last night and will immediately meet with He Yingqin to report on the situation in Shanxi Province and conduct some negotiations. (9th dispatch)

People from All Walks of Life in Beiping Commemorate the Fallen Soldiers 242

(Beiping) People from all walks of life in Beiping went to Tiananmen on the morning of the 9th to hold a meeting to commemorate the fallen soldiers. Several hundred people attended. (9th dispatch)

Tsinghua University's Ministry of Education Urges Payment 243

(Nanjing) Tsinghua University is facing financial difficulties due to the suspension of Boxer Indemnity payments and has overdrawn more than 200,000 yuan. President Mei Yiqi has requested the Ministry to quickly allocate 200,000 yuan. Zhu Jiahua replied by telegram that he has wired Song Ziwen of the Ministry of Finance to find a way.

(9th dispatch)

Washington Becomes the Center of World Politics 244

Roosevelt Invites Representatives of Various Countries to Discuss the Overall Situation

Separate Talks Will Be Held, Not a Round Table Meeting Format

Luther Appointed German Representative; France and Italy Are in the Process of Selecting

Reuters, London, 8th: The question of who will represent Germany, France, and Italy at the Washington conference to discuss economic matters is currently attracting the attention of various governments. The British Prime Minister is scheduled to depart for the United States on April 15th and will hold talks with President Roosevelt first. President Roosevelt has made it clear that he does not want to hold a round table conference in Washington but prefers to talk with representatives of various countries individually. According to news from Berlin, Dr. Luther, the German ambassador to the United States, and another member of the embassy will represent Germany. Dr. Luther is familiar with Germany's economic difficulties and world affairs, so the German cabinet selected him as its representative, so that German Chancellor Hitler or Foreign Minister Neurath may not have to travel to the US capital in person. The Italian government has not yet made a decision on sending an envoy to the United States, but it is generally expected that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, who has not left Italy since 1923, will probably not make a personal appearance. As for France, Foreign Minister Pang Gu today had a long telephone conversation with former Prime Minister Herriot. If Herriot accepts the government's invitation to represent France at the US meeting, the government will give him full authority and will not send a financial or economic delegation with him.

Aiming for Economic Compromise 245

Reuters, Washington, 8th: Secretary of State Hull told reporters today that the main goal of the United States in future economic discussions is to guide the world out of the predicament of economic nationalism. In recent years, various countries have revised their tariffs and engaged in competition, causing great harm. The United States is one of the creators of this situation and also one of the most severely affected. In the past few years, the United States has reduced its foreign trade by a huge amount of 600 million yuan. The goal of this discussion is to seek a general compromise on the principles of reducing tariffs and abolishing exchange restrictions. Due to time constraints, specific tariffs will be left to the countries themselves to determine. As for practical plans and detailed measures, they will be discussed at future world economic conferences. According to news today, Canada and Mexico have been invited by the United States to send personnel to the United States to participate in the discussions.

Japan Also Invited to Send Representative; Will Be Represented by Debuchi 246

Dentsu, Tokyo, September 9th: The United States is about to convene a preparatory meeting for the World Economic Conference. On the afternoon of the 7th, the Undersecretary of State verbally invited Ambassador Debuchi to the United States to participate on behalf of Japan. According to a telegram arriving at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the invitation included the following: "The President intends to personally discuss everything with the representatives of major countries regarding the preparation for the World Economic Conference and has issued invitations to various countries. This meeting will address the issue of disarmament, and it is hoped that your government will also send an important official as its representative." The Japanese government has decided to accept this offer and will instruct Ambassador Debuchi on the 10th to reply and participate in the meeting. The government representative must address the issues of war debts and disarmament, so it wants either Prime Minister Saitō or someone from the cabinet to go to the United States as its representative. However, it will be impossible to arrive in time for the preparatory meeting scheduled for the 22nd and 23rd. As a result, Ambassador Debuchi will be appointed, assisted by Finance Officer Tsushima. However, since the US President will meet with representatives of various countries separately, there is no need to arrive in the United States by the 22nd or 23rd. The possibility of sending another important official is being considered. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has instructed Ambassador Debuchi today to report in detail.

Dentsu, Tokyo, September 9th: The International Economic Conference will be held before July 25th. From June 10th, preparatory talks will first be held in Washington by major countries. The Japanese government, with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance at its center, will establish a committee to discuss countermeasures. The general policy that will be adopted is as follows: (1) Although the war debt issue is not directly related to Japan, Japan will fully support the economic conference to cooperate with various countries in overcoming the world's economic depression. However, on the issue of disarmament, Japan will adhere to its established policy, that is, adhere to the contents of the Japanese proposal submitted to the General Disarmament Committee in Geneva. (2) Regarding international economic policy, Japan will advocate the following points and demonstrate its practical coordination: (a) The international adjustment of commodity prices and economic problems should be based on the restoration of the gold standard. (b) Restore the price of silver. (c) In order to adjust the movement of capital, restrictions on exchange must be eased. (d) To ensure the freedom of commerce and make it thorough, international coordination should be conducted on tariff policies.

Deteriorating Relations Between Russia and the Puppet State Over the Chinese Eastern Railway Issue 247

(Harbin) The Soviet side prevented the western line of the Chinese Eastern Railway from directly connecting with the Trans-Baikal Railway at Manzhouli yesterday. It is heard that the Soviet side will take similar actions on the eastern line. The puppet Manchukuo side plans to take similar coercive action at Pogranichnaya, the point where the Ussuri and Eastern Railway lines connect, as it did at Manzhouli. Relations between Russia and "Manchukuo" are becoming increasingly strained due to the Soviet side's removal of freight cars. (Dentsu dispatch, 9th)

(Changchun) Disputes over the Chinese Eastern Railway issue are intensifying. Due to the Soviet side's actions, train operations are being hindered. Morita, the director of the puppet railway, has urgently traveled to Harbin again. Prior to his departure, Morita consulted with key officials of the State Council at 9 AM yesterday, and the following policies were decided: They will use this as the basis to make serious demands on Guziriev, the deputy director of the Chinese Eastern Railway: (1) The usage fee for all freight cars of the Chinese Eastern Railway used by the Soviet Union in the past year must be paid in the amount of 4 million gold rubles. (2) The date of payment must be clearly stated. (3) "Manchukuo" respects the existing treaties and believes that the management rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway are equal to each other according to the Feng-Soviet Agreement. (Dentsu dispatch, 9th)

British Hostility Towards Russia Deemed Inappropriate by Russian Newspaper 248

TASS, Inisk, England, 8th: The Soviet Union considers the British government's attitude towards the case of the British engineers of the Vickers Company being detained, as demonstrated by the recent passage of the authorization to the government to ban Russian goods, to be inappropriate. Today's government gazette "Izvestia" commented on it in an editorial. It said that after the British diplomatic authorities received the news that British engineers had been detained in the Soviet Union, without asking how the case was, they used all kinds of intimidation, proposing the theory that they could not have committed a crime. The Soviet government gave a careful reply to this kind of diplomatic intimidation. Because its purpose was not achieved, the British government increased its threat and made it a concrete proposal to threaten the Soviet Union with material losses. However, the Soviet industry is overthrowing the old Russia, not to create freedom on Soviet land for foreign capitalists, nor to introduce imperialist laws to its land. Therefore, the British government's threat in this case only shows the nature of its foreign policy. The British government, as one of the initiators of the future World Economic Conference, is a "restorer" of the world economy, and now it is creating a prominent example of damaging international relations. It is easy for foreigners to commit crimes in other countries, especially in the economic relations of two different social systems. If the British authorities want to threaten to sever business relations because of this kind of incident, it will be difficult to do business. In fact, there are thousands of foreign engineers in the Soviet Union, and only this kind of judicial interference occasionally occurs, which shows that the Soviet Union has no malice in it. The British government's threat of economic boycott in this kind of event, which is not a violation of international commercial treaties but only the application of law to foreign criminals in other countries, shows that Britain may have deeper motives. We will talk about this motive in the future. At present, what the Soviet Union wants to decide is how to apply its laws. The newspaper concluded that no matter how threatened, the Soviet court will not be affected. The only result of this kind of threat is to make the workers and peasants of the Soviet Union understand what the words of friendship and peace used in British diplomacy are worth. As for which of the British and Soviet Union will suffer greater losses due to this kind of threat, we will have to wait for future results.

German Arrest of Russian Nationals 249

German Ambassador to Moscow Assures Russia

Will Not Hinder Bilateral Business Relations

TASS, Moscow, 8th: German Ambassador Dirkson visited Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov today, stating that the German government has begun investigating the protest raised by the Soviet Union on April 3 regarding the illegal arrest and abuse of Russian nationals reported by the Soviet embassy. At the same time, Dirkson assured that the German government will ensure that Soviet business institutions can operate unhindered in accordance with the treaty. Regarding Dirkson's hope that Soviet business institutions can sever ties with the German Communist Party, and mentioning that a large number of German employees of the Delopro Company are Communists, Litvinov declared that Soviet business institutions are absolutely forbidden from having relations with the Communist Party or other political parties. They have received strict instructions not to interfere in Germany's internal affairs, so this kind of assumption has no factual basis. However, Soviet business institutions cannot be responsible for the individual political activities of their employees, especially since German institutions and companies are still allowed to employ Communists.

German Public Opinion Attaches Importance to Davis' Visit to Berlin; Seeks Equality in Disarmament 250

Havas, Berlin, 8th: German public opinion is paying close attention to the talks between Davis, the US Chief Representative to the Disarmament Conference, and President Hindenburg, Chancellor Hitler, and Foreign Minister Neurath. The Vossische Zeitung reported, "Regarding the World Economic Conference, what Germany hopes for is that several international financial issues can be resolved by the conference. This is well known to the world. As for the issue of disarmament, what Germany has been demanding for years is that other countries fulfill their contractual obligations and engage in disarmament. If other countries fail to fulfill their obligations, then Germany will decide on its course of action."

Havas, Berlin, 8th: The "Local Guidance" newspaper commented on the visit to Berlin by Davis, the US Chief Representative to the Disarmament Conference, saying, "The German government will tell Davis that Germany is only interested in true peace, and that the various difficulties encountered in the current political and economic situation cannot be eliminated unless the rights of all countries are equal."

German Government Bans Jews from Serving in Civil Administration 251

French Socialist Party Opposes German Anti-Jewish Movement

Marquess of Reading Resigns as President of the Anglo-German Association

German Communist Party Organs Searched

Reuters, Berlin, 8th: Today, the German government issued a new law that all Jews are forbidden from serving in civil administration. Therefore, tens of thousands of officials left over from the previous government will be dismissed. Only Jews who were already serving in civil administration when the European War began on August 1, 1914, and those who served in the trenches during the European War, or whose fathers and sons fought for Germany, may retain their positions. This number is very small. Anyone who has one Jew among their four grandparents will be considered a Jewish official. All Jews who obtained civil administration positions after 1918 solely because of joining a political party and without the necessary special qualifications will also be dismissed, receiving only three months' salary and no benefits.

Havas, Danzig, 8th: A group of armed National Socialists broke into a Jewish restaurant, beat and expelled customers with sticks, and smashed the windows before leaving.

Havas, Paris, 8th: Two rallies were held in Paris today to oppose the German anti-Jewish movement. Socialist leader Blum and many celebrities spoke. The crowd wanted to hold a demonstration, but the government forbade it. At the end of the meeting, a motion was passed stating, "The current German administration is sufficient to reduce its national status. We hereby strongly condemn it. We express our approval to anyone who morally and materially resists Germany under Hitler's rule." When the crowd dispersed, they shouted "Long live peace" and "Down with Hitler" slogans.

Reuters, London, 8th: British politician the Marquess of Reading, who has served as Viceroy of India and in key cabinet positions, has resigned as President of the Anglo-German Association and left the association because he is dissatisfied with the anti-Jewish policies currently adopted by the German government. The Marquess of Reading has been elected as President of the Anglo-German Association since 1929. Reuters, Breslau, 8th: Today, a tavern in Breslau started a fight because it sang an anti-Marxist war song, resulting in two deaths and two injuries. Subsequently, thousands of National Socialist stormtroopers searched houses door to door and arrested more than a hundred people, including several key members of the Communist Party. According to police officials, it has been determined that the Communist Party is trying to reorganize into a "terrorist group." During the search, a number of weapons were seized.

US Public Hoards Gold and Transports It Abroad; Disregards the Government's Stern Orders 252

Reuters, New York, 8th: The New York Commercial Bulletin stated that President Roosevelt has begun to use the power of the government to implement public works programs to settle the unemployed. President Roosevelt has rejected any plan to print unsecured banknotes and has limited the direct expansion of currency and the indirect expansion caused by the issuance of public works bonds. Most of those hoarding large amounts of cash in the United States have not sent their hidden gold to banks. In order to deal with these people, President Roosevelt will issue stern orders, only allowing cash to be used for necessary domestic and foreign commercial purposes, and this use must be certified by a license issued by the Ministry of Finance. Since the banking holiday last month, more than 600 million yuan in cash and gold certificates have returned to the banks, but 600 million yuan in gold coins and gold certificates still remain in the hands of the public and have not returned to the banks. It is heard that those hoarding the most gold are listening to lawyers' advice not to return the gold to the banks despite the President's orders. No matter how much is hidden, they are not entering the banks, or else they will be severely punished. Currently, some people are trying to test the constitutionality of this order. Constitutional experts believe that this test is one of the most interesting events in history, regarding whether the government has the power to confiscate private property. Many hoarders have already moved their gold to Europe and Canada. Although the authorities know who they are, they have not yet decided how to deal with the situation.

A Female Jockey Is As Good As Any Man 253

Havas, Maisons-Laffitte, France, 8th: In today's horse racing here, there were several races specifically for female jockeys. Eight participants were present, all wearing short jackets and riding breeches, dressed in green and red, shining in the sun. Their spirit was no less than any man. At the signal, eight steeds charged forward, racing like the wind and lightning, competing fiercely. Ms. Warren won the first and second races. Ms. Randall won the steeplechase race. After the female jockey race, their bodies were covered in sweat and their cheeks were flushed. The audience welcomed them enthusiastically. Today's results were good, so there will be more of these races next time.

American Representative Comes to China to Negotiate Direct Sino-American Flights 254

(Nanjing) The United American Corporation of the United States has sent a representative to China to negotiate direct Sino-American flights with China National Aviation Corporation. It is reported that the preliminary plan involves establishing a large-scale connecting aviation station in Alaska. The flight path would start from Alaska, pass through the Bering Sea and Siberia, and go directly to Shanghai, China. The Sino-American flight would take three days. If feasible, it is expected to be implemented in January next year. The China National Aviation Corporation has already submitted this plan to the Ministry for review. (9th Dispatch)

The Truth About Zhang Xueliang's Sale of the Naval Hospital, Announced by the Ministry of the Navy 255

(Nanjing) The Ministry of the Navy has announced the truth about Zhang Xueliang's sale of the Naval Hospital. The original text states that, before leaving for Beiping, Zhang arbitrarily and privately sold all the land and buildings of the Tianjin Hospital Medical School of the Ministry of the Navy to the French Concession authorities where the hospital and medical school were located, exceeding his authority. After the Ministry discovered this, it sent several telegrams to Zhang to stop him, but received no response. The French Concession authorities, based on the contract signed by Zhang, led French soldiers and police at the end of last month, forcibly occupied all the buildings of the school, relying on their strength. In addition to separately submitting requests to the highest military authorities and the Executive Yuan to initiate negotiations with the French side, it is imperative to achieve the cancellation of this illegal contract of confusing the jurisdiction system and selling beyond authority, and to return the original property to the Navy Department before stopping. (9th Dispatch)

Zhang Ji Telegrams Wu Tiecheng to Request the Seizure of Ancient Calligraphy and Paintings from the Summer Palace 256

(Nanjing) Because Zhang Xueliang is about to go abroad, Zhang Ji telegraphed Wu Tiecheng on the 8th to inquire about the ancient calligraphy and paintings of the Summer Palace, requesting that they be detained as appropriate. The original telegram reads: "Respectfully to Mayor Wu of the Shanghai Municipal Government, and to all newspapers: Having read in the newspaper that Zhang Xueliang is about to travel abroad by boat, although the bronzes of the Summer Palace have already been transported south, many of the ancient calligraphy and paintings of the garden are in Zhang Xueliang's hands. It is appropriate to inspect and detain them as soon as possible, so that the national treasures will not be lost overseas. I would be most grateful. Zhang Ji, Jia." (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Tianjin Hosts International Football Match, Chinese Team Wins Right to Final 257

(Tianjin) The Elrod International Football Tournament opened at 3:00 PM on the 8th at the British Field. The Chinese team played against the World team, with approximately 5,000 spectators. In the first half, the World team won 2-0. In the second half, the Chinese team won 4-0, securing the right to the final. The second group's semi-final match, the British team versus the Russian team, is scheduled for 3:00 PM on the 9th. After this battle is resolved, the final battle is scheduled for the 17th. However, because the Chinese team will play the Shanghai team on the 15th and 16th, they have decided to request a postponement from the All China Football Federation. The Chinese team's lineup is as follows: Chen Erde, Wang Hongrong, Jin Adu, Fu Xinqiu, Sun Sijing, Liang Mingzong, Jiang Lu, Bai Qingguo, Zhang Changyu, Yu Guohua, Zhao Qixiang. (9th Dispatch)

Recent Railway Engineering Statistics 258

(Nanjing) In recent years, despite the national government's financial difficulties, it has still worked hard to plan road construction and has achieved some success. The following is a report on the recent achievements in railway engineering across the country: (A) Roads completed from 1929 to 1932: (1) National-operated Lingtong Section, 72 kilometers, Kaile Section 50 kilometers, Tongguan Huayin Section 24 kilometers; (2) Provincial-operated Su Shan-Lanxi Section 200 kilometers, totaling 346 kilometers. (B) Currently under construction or preparing to start construction: (1) National-operated Lechang to Dashimen 45 kilometers, Huayin to Weinan 49 kilometers, Yuci to Taigu 35 kilometers, Taigu to Pingyao 45 kilometers; (2) Provincial-operated Jinhua to Yushan 155 kilometers; (3) Privately-operated Wuhu to Sunjiabu, 81 kilometers, totaling 441 kilometers under construction. (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)
